   }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Kafka consumer offset management is implemented across multiple layers in the apache/kafka repository. The core offset storage and management is handled in the group-coordinator module. OffsetAndMetadata (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) represents a committed offset with its metadata, leaderEpoch, and timestamp. The offset storage in __consumer_offsets is managed through OffsetMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java), which handles the request processing and replay of offset records. This manager contains methods like handleCommitOffsets, handleFetchOffsets, handleDeleteOffsets, and handleTxnCommitOffsets that process offset commits, fetches, deletions, and transactional commits. The GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the high-level API for offset operations including commitOffsets, fetchOffsets, fetchAllOffsets, deleteOffsets, and commitTransactionalOffsets. The GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) is the replicated state machine that implements the GroupCoordinator interface and handles offset commit/fetch requests from clients. Offset expiry is managed through OffsetExpirationCondition (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java) and OffsetExpirationConditionImpl (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java), which determine when offsets should be expired based on group state and retention time. Classic consumer groups use ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java), while modern consumer groups use ConsumerGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java). Both group types support offset storage backed by records in the __consumer_offsets partition. Offset records are defined in JSON schemas: OffsetCommitKey.json, OffsetCommitValue.json, LegacyOffsetCommitKey.json, and LegacyOffsetCommitValue.json. On the client side, OffsetAndMetadata (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java) is the client-facing representation of offset metadata. CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles offset commit operations on the consumer client, while OffsetFetcher (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetFetcher.java) handles fetching offsets. Admin client operations for offset management are provided through handlers: ListConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/internals/ListConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.java), AlterConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/internals/AlterConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.java), and DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler. Request and response classes for offset operations include OffsetCommitRequest, OffsetCommitResponse, OffsetFetchRequest, OffsetFetchResponse, TxnOffsetCommitRequest, and TxnOffsetCommitResponse. The complete offset management architecture integrates offset commit/fetch handlers in GroupCoordinatorShard with the OffsetMetadataManager for storage, expiry logic through OffsetExpirationCondition, and client-side coordination through CommitRequestManager and OffsetFetcher.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1054,"cache_read_input_tokens":62071,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1054},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"1765f1be-d99f-42ec-9dcd-79f58eeeb40b","uuid":"22b2a0da-e61e-44e4-8071-92752cae6398"}

   }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Kafka consumer offset management is implemented across multiple layers in the apache/kafka repository. The core offset storage and management is handled in the group-coordinator module. OffsetAndMetadata (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java) represents a committed offset with its metadata, leaderEpoch, and timestamp. The offset storage in __consumer_offsets is managed through OffsetMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java), which handles the request processing and replay of offset records. This manager contains methods like handleCommitOffsets, handleFetchOffsets, handleDeleteOffsets, and handleTxnCommitOffsets that process offset commits, fetches, deletions, and transactional commits. The GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the high-level API for offset operations including commitOffsets, fetchOffsets, fetchAllOffsets, deleteOffsets, and commitTransactionalOffsets. The GroupCoordinatorShard (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java) is the replicated state machine that implements the GroupCoordinator interface and handles offset commit/fetch requests from clients. Offset expiry is managed through OffsetExpirationCondition (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java) and OffsetExpirationConditionImpl (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java), which determine when offsets should be expired based on group state and retention time. Classic consumer groups use ClassicGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java), while modern consumer groups use ConsumerGroup (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java). Both group types support offset storage backed by records in the __consumer_offsets partition. Offset records are defined in JSON schemas: OffsetCommitKey.json, OffsetCommitValue.json, LegacyOffsetCommitKey.json, and LegacyOffsetCommitValue.json. On the client side, OffsetAndMetadata (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java) is the client-facing representation of offset metadata. CommitRequestManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CommitRequestManager.java) handles offset commit operations on the consumer client, while OffsetFetcher (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/OffsetFetcher.java) handles fetching offsets. Admin client operations for offset management are provided through handlers: ListConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/internals/ListConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.java), AlterConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/admin/internals/AlterConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler.java), and DeleteConsumerGroupOffsetsHandler. Request and response classes for offset operations include OffsetCommitRequest, OffsetCommitResponse, OffsetFetchRequest, OffsetFetchResponse, TxnOffsetCommitRequest, and TxnOffsetCommitResponse. The complete offset management architecture integrates offset commit/fetch handlers in GroupCoordinatorShard with the OffsetMetadataManager for storage, expiry logic through OffsetExpirationCondition, and client-side coordination through CommitRequestManager and OffsetFetcher.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
